FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
        WHERE [m1].[Id] = [m0].[Id]) AS [Url], [r].[Id]
    FROM [RoleMenuPermission] AS [r]
    INNER JOIN [Menu] AS [m0] ON [r].[SubMenuId] = [m0].[Id]
    WHERE [r].[RoleId] = @__roleId_0 AND [m].[Id] = [r].[MenuId]
) AS [t]
WHERE [m].[ParentId] = N'0'

    SELECT TOP(1) [c].[Id], [c].[Address], [c].[CardGuid], [c].[CityId], [c].[CityName], [c].[CommunityId], [c].[CommunityName], [c].[CommunityTypeId], [c].[CreatedBy], [c].[CreatedDate], [c].[FeesMonthly], [c].[GracePeriod], [c].[NoOfParkingLot], [c].[NoOfUnits], [c].[PICEmail], [c].[PICMobile], [c].[PICName], [c].[StateId], [c].[UpdatedBy], [c].[UpdatedDate], [s].[Id] AS [Id0], [s].[Name], [c0].[Id] AS [Id1], [c0].[Name] AS [Name0], [c0].[StateId] AS [StateId0]

    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]

SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Name], [m].[Url], [t].[SubmenuId], [t].[SubmenuName], [t].[Url], [t].[Id]
FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
        WHERE [m1].[Id] = [m0].[Id]) AS [Url], [r].[Id]
    FROM [RoleMenuPermission] AS [r]
    INNER JOIN [Menu] AS [m0] ON [r].[SubMenuId] = [m0].[Id]
    WHERE [r].[RoleId] = @__roleId_0 AND [m].[Id] = [r].[MenuId]
) AS [t]
WHERE [m].[ParentId] = N'0'
ORDER BY [m].[Id], [t].[Id]

SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Name], [m].[Url], [t].[SubmenuId], [t].[SubmenuName], [t].[Url], [t].[Id]
FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
        WHERE [m1].[Id] = [m0].[Id]) AS [Url], [r].[Id]
    FROM [RoleMenuPermission] AS [r]
    INNER JOIN [Menu] AS [m0] ON [r].[SubMenuId] = [m0].[Id]
    WHERE [r].[RoleId] = @__roleId_0 AND [m].[Id] = [r].[MenuId]
) AS [t]
WHERE [m].[ParentId] = N'0'
ORDER BY [m].[Id], [t].[Id]

FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (

SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Name], [m].[Url], [t].[SubmenuId], [t].[SubmenuName], [t].[Url], [t].[Id]
FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
        WHERE [m1].[Id] = [m0].[Id]) AS [Url], [r].[Id]
    FROM [RoleMenuPermission] AS [r]
    INNER JOIN [Menu] AS [m0] ON [r].[SubMenuId] = [m0].[Id]
    WHERE [r].[RoleId] = @__roleId_0 AND [m].[Id] = [r].[MenuId]
) AS [t]
WHERE [m].[ParentId] = N'0'
ORDER BY [m].[Id], [t].[Id]

FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]

FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (

SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Name], [m].[Url], [t].[SubmenuId], [t].[SubmenuName], [t].[Url], [t].[Id]
FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
        WHERE [m1].[Id] = [m0].[Id]) AS [Url], [r].[Id]

    INNER JOIN [Menu] AS [m0] ON [r].[SubMenuId] = [m0].[Id]

) AS [t]
WHERE [m].[ParentId] = N'0'
ORDER BY [m].[Id], [t].[Id]

SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Name], [m].[Url], [t].[SubmenuId], [t].[SubmenuName], [t].[Url], [t].[Id]
FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
        WHERE [m1].[Id] = [m0].[Id]) AS [Url], [r].[Id]
    FROM [RoleMenuPermission] AS [r]
    INNER JOIN [Menu] AS [m0] ON [r].[SubMenuId] = [m0].[Id]
    WHERE [r].[RoleId] = @__roleId_0 AND [m].[Id] = [r].[MenuId]
) AS [t]
WHERE [m].[ParentId] = N'0'
ORDER BY [m].[Id], [t].[Id]

SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Name], [m].[Url], [t].[SubmenuId], [t].[SubmenuName], [t].[Url], [t].[Id]
FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
        WHERE [m1].[Id] = [m0].[Id]) AS [Url], [r].[Id]
    FROM [RoleMenuPermission] AS [r]
    INNER JOIN [Menu] AS [m0] ON [r].[SubMenuId] = [m0].[Id]
    WHERE [r].[RoleId] = @__roleId_0 AND [m].[Id] = [r].[MenuId]
) AS [t]
WHERE [m].[ParentId] = N'0'
ORDER BY [m].[Id], [t].[Id]

SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Name], [m].[Url], [t].[SubmenuId], [t].[SubmenuName], [t].[Url], [t].[Id]
FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
        WHERE [m1].[Id] = [m0].[Id]) AS [Url], [r].[Id]
    FROM [RoleMenuPermission] AS [r]
    INNER JOIN [Menu] AS [m0] ON [r].[SubMenuId] = [m0].[Id]
    WHERE [r].[RoleId] = @__roleId_0 AND [m].[Id] = [r].[MenuId]
) AS [t]
WHERE [m].[ParentId] = N'0'
ORDER BY [m].[Id], [t].[Id]

SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Name], [m].[Url], [t].[SubmenuId], [t].[SubmenuName], [t].[Url], [t].[Id]
FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
        WHERE [m1].[Id] = [m0].[Id]) AS [Url], [r].[Id]
    FROM [RoleMenuPermission] AS [r]
    INNER JOIN [Menu] AS [m0] ON [r].[SubMenuId] = [m0].[Id]
    WHERE [r].[RoleId] = @__roleId_0 AND [m].[Id] = [r].[MenuId]
) AS [t]
WHERE [m].[ParentId] = N'0'

FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
        WHERE [m1].[Id] = [m0].[Id]) AS [Url], [r].[Id]

SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Name], [m].[Url], [t].[SubmenuId], [t].[SubmenuName], [t].[Url], [t].[Id]
FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
        WHERE [m1].[Id] = [m0].[Id]) AS [Url], [r].[Id]
    FROM [RoleMenuPermission] AS [r]
    INNER JOIN [Menu] AS [m0] ON [r].[SubMenuId] = [m0].[Id]
    WHERE [r].[RoleId] = @__roleId_0 AND [m].[Id] = [r].[MenuId]
) AS [t]
WHERE [m].[ParentId] = N'0'
ORDER BY [m].[Id], [t].[Id]

SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Name], [m].[Url], [t].[SubmenuId], [t].[SubmenuName], [t].[Url], [t].[Id]
FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
        WHERE [m1].[Id] = [m0].[Id]) AS [Url], [r].[Id]
    FROM [RoleMenuPermission] AS [r]
    INNER JOIN [Menu] AS [m0] ON [r].[SubMenuId] = [m0].[Id]
    WHERE [r].[RoleId] = @__roleId_0 AND [m].[Id] = [r].[MenuId]
) AS [t]
WHERE [m].[ParentId] = N'0'
ORDER BY [m].[Id], [t].[Id]

SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Name], [m].[Url], [t].[SubmenuId], [t].[SubmenuName], [t].[Url], [t].[Id]
FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
        WHERE [m1].[Id] = [m0].[Id]) AS [Url], [r].[Id]
    FROM [RoleMenuPermission] AS [r]
    INNER JOIN [Menu] AS [m0] ON [r].[SubMenuId] = [m0].[Id]
    WHERE [r].[RoleId] = @__roleId_0 AND [m].[Id] = [r].[MenuId]
) AS [t]
WHERE [m].[ParentId] = N'0'
ORDER BY [m].[Id], [t].[Id]

FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]

FROM [Resident] AS [r]
LEFT JOIN [State] AS [s] ON [r].[StateId] = [s].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [r0].[Id], [r0].[Amount], [r0].[CreatedBy], [r0].[CreatedDate], [r0].[PaymentDate], [r0].[PaymentRef], [r0].[PaymentStatusId], [r0].[PaymentTypeId], [r0].[ResidentId], [r0].[UpdatedBy], [r0].[UpdatedDate], [p].[Id] AS [Id0], [p].[CreatedBy] AS [CreatedBy0], [p].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [p].[Name], [p].[UpdatedBy] AS [UpdatedBy0], [p].[UpdatedDate] AS [UpdatedDate0]
    FROM [ResidencePaymentDetails] AS [r0]
    INNER JOIN [PaymentStatus] AS [p] ON [r0].[PaymentStatusId] = [p].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [r].[Id] = [t].[ResidentId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [r1].[Id], [r1].[Amount], [r1].[CreatedBy], [r1].[CreatedDate], [r1].[PaymentDate], [r1].[PaymentRef], [r1].[PaymentStatusId], [r1].[PaymentTypeId], [r1].[ResidentId], [r1].[UpdatedBy], [r1].[UpdatedDate], [p0].[Id] AS [Id0], [p0].[CreatedBy] AS [CreatedBy0], [p0].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [p0].[Name], [p0].[UpdatedBy] AS [UpdatedBy0], [p0].[UpdatedDate] AS [UpdatedDate0]
    FROM [ResidencePaymentDetails] AS [r1]
    INNER JOIN [PaymentStatus] AS [p0] ON [r1].[PaymentStatusId] = [p0].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [r].[Id] = [t0].[ResidentId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [t2].[PaymentDate], [t2].[Amount], [t2].[PaymentStatusName], [t2].[c], [t2].[ResidentId]
    FROM (
        SELECT [r2].[PaymentDate], [r2].[Amount], [p1].[Name] AS [PaymentStatusName], 1 AS [c], [r2].[ResidentId], ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY [r2].[ResidentId] ORDER BY [r2].[Id], [p1].[Id]) AS [row]
        FROM [ResidencePaymentDetails] AS [r2]
        INNER JOIN [PaymentStatus] AS [p1] ON [r2].[PaymentStatusId] = [p1].[Id]
        WHERE ([r2].[PaymentDate] IS NOT NULL) AND DATEPART(month, [r2].[PaymentDate]) = @__currentMonth_1 AND DATEPART(year, [r2].[PaymentDate]) = @__currentYear_2
    ) AS [t2]
    WHERE [t2].[row] <= 1
) AS [t1] ON [r].[Id] = [t1].[ResidentId]
WHERE [r].[CommunityId] = @__communityId_0
ORDER BY [r].[Id], [s].[Id], [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [t0].[Id]
